"26. 直角刚杆AO＝2m，BO＝3m，如图4-2-15所示。已知某瞬时A点的速度v<sub>A</sub>＝6m/s，而B点的加速度与BO成θ＝60°角。则该瞬时刚杆的角加速度α为{{c1::（）}}rad/s2。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""206"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/80182305-e760-4b5f-8380-f211f56bd8bd.jpg"" width=""295""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-2-15</span>"	"3<br><img height=""19"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1d8f4962-53d0-47df-ba6b-37f01be8556a.png"" width=""24""/><br><img height=""19"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a3bf87c3-da46-482e-b5f5-1bd9dc4cb366.png"" width=""37""/><br><img height=""21"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1e6f9918-78ea-4993-b7dc-e088566f48c4.png"" width=""35""/>"	D	"由题意可得，刚杆的角速度为：<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/fa7649d4-af09-4df6-bd83-6fe13726eeae.png"" width=""118""/>则B点法向加速度为：<img height=""27"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/86538f03-b6ae-48ed-a764-0e6840025a42.png"" width=""139""/>又B点加速度a是<img height=""23"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f389e698-4477-4992-a868-b6c06bd98296.jpg"" width=""67""/>的合加速度，故有：<img height=""48"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0bc4a6da-e698-4d68-9b30-90e5833c09d0.jpg"" width=""79""/>，则<img height=""27"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b2bfbea4-05ab-4905-ab9c-503c874ac893.jpg"" width=""196""/>，瞬时刚杆的角加速度为：<img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8bb46cc1-5e2e-4920-b6fc-209f5440199c.jpg"" width=""149""/>。"	
"27. 如图4-2-16所示，半径为R的半圆形凸轮以匀速u沿水平向右运动，带动从动杆AB沿铅直方向运动，则当φ＝30°时，A点相对于凸轮的速度为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""253"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/eb995e3d-207e-4359-bbe5-d34981590cae.jpg"" width=""281""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-2-16</span>"	"<img height=""44"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a3dd36a6-2b96-4164-bcf3-764ff10d5732.jpg"" width=""27""/>A的切线方向，指左上<br>u，水平指右<br><img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a3197380-9304-42d1-b95e-497a09eb9e69.jpg"" width=""22""/>，A的切线方向，指左上<br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/05e7a9ec-a1c4-4931-8397-fba11437cccc.jpg"" width=""21""/>，A的切线方向，指左上"	D	"取杆AB的A点为动点，凸轮为动参考系。杆AB做平动，动点A的绝对运动是跟AB的直线运动，相对运动是以凸轮圆心O为圆心、半径为R的逆时针圆周运动。动点A相对凸轮水平向速度为v<sub>x</sub>=u（左），即沿圆周切向速度v的水平分量，其竖向分量v<sub>y</sub>即动点A的绝度运动速度。作v的分解图示可得，<img height=""46"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bdca2ba8-631f-4d0a-8e05-71eb6891c291.png"" width=""192""/>"	
"28. 长L的直杆OA，以角速度ω绕O轴转动，杆的A端铰接一个半径为r的圆盘，圆盘相对于直杆以角速度ωr绕A轴转动，如图4-2-17所示。今以圆盘边缘上的一点M为动点，OA为动坐标，当AM垂直OA时，M点的牵连速度为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""295"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6151bbf8-6cba-440d-8de3-1ccd2afb61a6.png"" width=""293""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-2-17</span>"	v<sub>e</sub>=Lω，方向沿AM<br>v<sub>e</sub>=rω，方向垂直AM，指向左下方<br>v<sub>e</sub>=（L<sup>2</sup>+r<sup>2</sup>）<sup>1/2</sup>ω，方向垂直OM，指向右下方<br>v<sub>e</sub>=L（ω-ω<sub>r</sub>），方向沿AM	C	某点的牵连速度即为动系中与该点重合的那一点的速度。M点与系统转动中心O的距离为（L<sup>2</sup>+r<sup>2</sup>）<sup>1/2</sup>，因此M点的牵连速度为：ve=（L<sup>2</sup>+r<sup>2</sup>）<sup>1/2</sup>ω，方向由角速度方向可知为垂直于OM并指向右下方。	
"29. 小车沿水平方向向右作加速运动，其加速度a<sub>0</sub>=49.2cm/s<sup>2</sup>，在小车上有一轮绕O轴转动，转动规律为φ=t<sup>2</sup>（t以秒计，φ以弧度计）。当t=1s时，轮缘上点A的位置如图4-2-18所示。如轮的半径r＝20cm，则此时点A的绝对加速度aA为{{c1::（）}}cm/s<sup>2</sup>。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""211"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/843cdb06-ec94-437f-be69-657e34b6f410.jpg"" width=""257""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-2-18</span>"	24.7<br>43.5<br>68.2<br>74.6	D	"当t=1s时，A点绕O点转动的角速度<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/80418cd7-b113-4b59-aa52-d33f2ac371b9.jpg"" width=""124""/>角加速度<img height=""43"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6aa547ec-7ca5-4447-9290-a93a4a73ffd1.jpg"" width=""133""/>。<br/>于是A点相对于小车的加速度为：a<sub>n</sub>=rω<sup>2</sup>=80cm/s2，a<sub>τ</sub>=rα=40cm/s<sup>2</sup>。<br/>可得A点绝对加速度分量为：a<sub>V</sub>=a<sub>τ</sub>cos30°+ansin30°=74.6cm/s<sup>2</sup>，a<sub>H</sub>=a<sub>0</sub>+a<sub>τ</sub>sin30°-ancos30°=0。<br/>则可得点A的绝对加速度a<sub>A</sub>为：<img height=""27"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b860c60a-57cf-4c3d-afd3-edde007cf44f.jpg"" width=""210""/>。"	
1. 重为W的货物由电梯载运下降，当电梯加速下降，匀速下降及减速下降时，货物对地板的压力分别为R<sub>1</sub>、R<sub>2</sub>、R<sub>3</sub>，它们之间的关系为{{c1::（）}}。[2010年真题]	R<sub>1</sub>=R<sub>2</sub>=R<sub>3</sub><br>R<sub>1</sub>>R<sub>2</sub>>R<sub>3</sub><br>R<sub>1</sub><R<sub>2</sub><R<sub>3</sub><br>R<sub>1</sub><R<sub>2</sub>>R<sub>3</sub>	C	根据牛顿运动定律F=ma，加速下降 a向下，匀速下降a等于0，减速下降 a向上；设货物对地板的压力为R<sub>i</sub>，i为1、2、3，而W-R<sub>i</sub>=ma，a以向下为正，向上为负，故R<sub>1</sub><R<sub>2</sub><R<sub>3</sub>。	
"2. 图4-3-1所示均质链条传动机构的大齿轮以角速度ω转动，已知大齿轮半径为R，质量为m<sub>1</sub>，小齿轮半径为r，质量为m<sub>2</sub>，链条质量不计，则此系统的动量为{{c1::（）}}。[2014年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""127"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4a34c15f-4ce9-4ad6-ab86-2e4111952933.png"" width=""278""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-1</span>"	（m<sub>1</sub>+2m<sub>2</sub>）v（→）<br>（m<sub>1</sub>+m<sub>2</sub>）v（→）<br>（2m<sub>2</sub>-m<sub>1</sub>）v（→）<br>0	D	把两个齿轮看成是一个系统，总体来说整个系统都处于静止状态，速度为0，因此，根据动量的定义可知，整个系统的动量为0。	
"3. 图4-3-2所示均质圆轮，质量为m，半径为r，在铅垂面内绕通过圆盘中心O的水平轴以匀角速度ω转动。则系统动量、对中心O的动量矩、动能的大小为{{c1::（）}}。[2011年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""170"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/727f7634-3b25-42d3-b875-7d0e18faa782.png"" width=""192""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-2</span>"	"<img height=""37"" id=""图片 1"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/97e939cf-0284-4146-ba18-85b9aedd8b3f.png"" width=""159""/><br><img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1abff035-a4d2-4c8c-b005-ba7d3139b66f.png"" width=""180""/><br><img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d1e3e7f1-d92d-4362-9b63-86a9162c24d7.png"" width=""159""/><br><img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ab55ecef-a5eb-479a-ab30-b3e927e7c8a0.png"" width=""169""/>"	A	"动量是物体的质量与其速度的乘积，对于质点来说，p=mv；对于质点系来说，p=∑m<sub>i</sub>v<sub>i</sub>=mvC。由于该系统，v<sub>C</sub>=0，故系统动量为0。转动刚体的动量矩是刚体转动惯量与角速度的乘积，即L<sub>z</sub>=J<sub>z</sub>ω；而薄圆盘的转动惯量为：<img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ec49a2d1-4569-4a7b-abfd-66f164987ca2.jpg"" width=""74""/>。故而对中心O的动量矩为<img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/04889f00-345c-4be2-b205-d4b8c52a72c4.jpg"" width=""163""/>。又对于转动刚体，动能是刚体的转动惯量与角速度的平方之半，即<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/eb2eb1cc-4eb8-4f96-b2e0-82ec1405a234.jpg"" width=""267""/>。"	
"4. 如图4-3-3所示，两重物M1和M2的质量分别为m1和m2，二重物系在不计重量的软绳上，绳绕过均质定滑轮，滑轮半径为r，质量为M，则此滑轮系统的动量矩为{{c1::（）}}。[2011年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""232"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0913a6fc-5548-4cf2-8f7e-5abc34c65717.png"" width=""200""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-3</span>"	"<img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/3bfb57a8-b7bf-4f8e-b7b5-69f62ab54762.png"" width=""162""/><br><img height=""22"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e6111056-c7dd-4a5f-8173-630ce90721ac.png"" width=""119""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c68208a9-fbce-48b2-89b3-fd5380253817.png"" width=""157""/><br><img height=""21"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1fcf85c0-0b84-47f7-9e6a-0140992301dd.png"" width=""115""/>"	C	"滑轮体系对O点动量矩公式为：<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2016-07-26/60bdce70-c3aa-4bc3-9a43-b1636552895a.png"" title=""1.png""/>；<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2016-07-26/1ad40b6d-65e0-4b13-83a0-212861f02a1c.png"" title=""2.png""/>和<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2016-07-26/650ac5b7-1345-47ed-b44e-ceb91e34e22c.png"" title=""3.png""/>速度均为v，定滑轮的动量矩为<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2016-07-26/900c4575-a545-4788-a1f8-c72f28686c94.png"" title=""4.png""/>，所以<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2016-07-26/d0e5044b-16fa-411c-810d-48161731acd4.png"" title=""5.png""/>，三者方向一致，均为顺时针。"	
"5. 均质细杆AB重P、长2L，A端铰支，B端用绳系住，处于水平位置，如图4-3-4所示。当B端绳突然剪断瞬时，AB杆的角加速度的大小为{{c1::（）}}。[2011年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""135"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e4cb3fef-21d5-47ea-a439-134abf8a3a46.jpg"" width=""241""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-4</span>"	"0<br><img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f0e2bf8b-508a-45d6-ae0f-473be995d548.png"" width=""24""/><br><img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4ecdf19a-272e-4608-9d59-498c200821f4.png"" width=""22""/><br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/06adf3f7-1fe2-443f-85f3-fadc54f62b70.png"" width=""21""/>"	B	"由动量矩定理，对于定轴转动刚体，有J<sub>z</sub>α=∑Mz（F<sup>（e）</sup>）。由题可得：<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/587c4d68-224b-4d3d-b1a6-44fa0f1462f5.png"" width=""218""/>故得：<img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1e6d3fb6-8a8e-4ba7-9f54-9a9abd5dabf4.jpg"" width=""41""/>。"

"7. A块与B块叠放如图4-3-6所示，各接触面处均考虑摩擦。当B块受力F作用沿水平面运动时，A块仍静止于B块上，于是{{c1::（）}}。[2013年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""97"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bf1b58a7-4b52-41d6-813d-ae7195b8b5c7.png"" width=""237""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-6</span>"	各接触面处的摩擦力都作负功<br>各接触面处的摩擦力都作正功<br>A块上的摩擦力作正功<br>B块上的摩擦力作正功	C	力所做的功等于力与沿力的作用方向上位移的乘积，可见，A与B之间的摩擦力做正功，B与地面之间的摩擦力做负功。	
"8. 质量为m，长为2l的均质杆初始位于水平位置，如图4-3-7所示，A端脱落后，杆绕轴B转动，当杆转到铅垂位置时，AB杆B处的约束力大小为{{c1::（）}}。[2010年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""177"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/36d37b38-249b-4dee-8176-4ca91ea3a661.jpg"" width=""331""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-7</span>"	"F<sub>Bx</sub>=0；F<sub>By</sub>=0<br>F<sub>B</sub>x=0；<img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4b93375b-ff19-465e-a83f-6e34231fb539.jpg"" width=""63""/><br>F<sub>Bx</sub>=l；F<sub>By</sub>=mg<br>F<sub>Bx</sub>=0；<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-02-16/bfb1694f-d0e8-4cb1-a096-c69b46b76447.jpg"" title=""3.jpg""/>"	D	"根据机械能守恒定律，<img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f7c860ee-7cea-4ea8-9273-ffefe52c555a.png"" width=""287""/>则到达铅垂位置时向心加速度为<img height=""30"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ad4a0e0d-ada4-4c9d-9a73-25328c6bcccb.jpg"" width=""56""/>。根据达朗贝尔原理，<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/071609de-6bfc-4382-8e94-180250b96d4f.png"" width=""137""/>又水平方向合力为零，得F<sub>Bx</sub>=0。"	
"9. 质量为ｍ，长为2l的均质细杆初始位于水平位置，如图4-3-8所示。A端脱落后，杆绕轴B转动，当杆转到铅垂位置时，AB杆角加速度的大小为{{c1::（）}}。[2009年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""156"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6fe6a4ab-e3bc-49ce-bb0f-9afae13e2a9f.png"" width=""237""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-8</span>"	"0<br><img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/89faa8cf-3af0-43c5-9d25-e8581ec2f5a6.png"" width=""20""/><br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/cb13981a-4dc7-49cb-9743-e784da6b5b82.png"" width=""19""/><br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5d65e359-0e69-4368-a56a-d61d84182842.png"" width=""23""/>"	A	"根据机械能守恒定律，以B点所在水平线为参考，则初始机械能为零。最终时刻机械能=<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8f22ea2d-d601-4537-b0ee-174092e2d04b.jpg"" width=""348""/>，解得，<img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/47eb889b-dd46-4221-9544-0573f7512efa.jpg"" width=""73""/>为常数。故AB杆角加速度的大小为0。"	
"10. 质量不计的水平细杆AB长为L，在铅垂图面内绕A轴转动，其另一段固连质量为m的质点B，在图4-3-9所示水平位置静止释放，则此瞬时质点B的惯性力为{{c1::（）}}。[2014年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""72"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/90d812bf-7e83-4f40-b5a6-d9cee796df2e.png"" width=""223""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-9</span>"	"<img height=""25"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8c5acc5f-598c-4a5c-8b1f-acb8519a2f4a.png"" width=""55""/><br><img height=""25"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/72a9373d-93ad-4be2-adc3-ca760c2bb66c.png"" width=""73""/><br>0<br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bc691d9f-1973-4cad-96f7-02c3a1704943.png"" width=""74""/>"	A	质点惯性力的大小等于质点的质量与加速度的乘积。在水平位置静止释放的瞬时速度和角速度都为0，因此质点只有一个重力加速度g，惯性力的大小为mg。	
"11. 质量为m，半径为R的均质圆轮，绕垂直于图面的水平轴O转动，其角速度为ω。在图4-3-10所示瞬时，角加速度为0，轮心C在其最低位置，此时将圆轮的惯性力系向O点简化，其惯性力主矢和惯性力主矩的大小分别为{{c1::（）}}。[2013年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""125"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/478e6171-c488-4fef-b472-4c1bf3ff6704.jpg"" width=""206""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-10</span>"	"<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ce349828-8b99-46a4-a366-ce9bb6e750f1.jpg"" width=""52""/>，0<br>mRω<sup>2</sup>，0<br>0，0<br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b0de6873-cb0d-4673-b530-eb96ae475f6f.jpg"" width=""94""/>"	A	"因角加速度为0，故质心处无切向加速度，法向加速度大小为<img height=""32"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a568e5f6-285a-4b8e-9bf3-1040364a9ea5.jpg"" width=""32""/>，故惯性力大小为<img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6683aaa9-7a90-4110-89ba-9d720a7798cf.jpg"" width=""51""/>，方向竖直向下，作用线通过O点。所以惯性力主矢大小为<img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0b2f4269-e45c-4272-a92d-d71e61bd9f4c.jpg"" width=""51""/>，主矩为零。"

17. 质量为110kg的机器固定在刚度为2×10<sup>6</sup>N/m的弹性基础上，当系统发生共振时，机器的工作频率为{{c1::（）}}。[2013年真题]	66.7rad/s<br>95.3rad/s<br>42.6rad/s<br>134.8rad/s	D	"共振时，机器的工作频率与固有频率相等，由固有频率公式有：<img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d80f9ee2-8c17-4c89-a76a-3d95bbfbe880.jpg"" width=""242""/>。"	
18. 已知单自由度系统振动的固有频率ω<sub>0</sub>=2rad/s，若在其上分别作用幅值相同而频率为ω<sub>1</sub>=1rad/s、ω<sub>2</sub>=2rad/s、ω<sub>3</sub>=3rad/s的简谐干扰力，则此系统强迫振动的振幅为{{c1::（）}}。[2012年真题]	ω<sub>1</sub>=1rad/s时振幅最大<br>ω<sub>2</sub>=2rad/s时振幅最大<br>ω<sub>3</sub>=3rad/s振幅最大<br>不能确定	B	根据共振的原理，当干扰力的频率等于固有频率w<sub>0</sub>时，发生共振，此时振幅最大。	
"19. 图4-3-17所示装置中，已知质量m=200kg，弹簧刚度k=100N/cm，则图中各装置的振动周期为{{c1::（）}}。[2011年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""223"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/9ea0db0b-4be6-40d4-97f4-a94ed872600a.jpg"" width=""221""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-17</span>"	图（a）装置振动周期最大<br>图（b）装置振动周期最大<br>图（c）装置振动周期最大<br>三种装置振动周期相等	B	"图（a）弹簧为并联，等效弹簧刚度为2k，则系统的固有频率为：<img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d13ef41f-905f-401e-a658-8b01bf01f783.jpg"" width=""63""/>。<br/>图（b）弹簧为串联，等效弹簧刚度为<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5453f35a-d5f0-47af-86c7-8388437904e9.jpg"" width=""68""/>，则系统的固有频率为：<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6be9368d-4ba3-4743-8537-e411d507ada3.jpg"" width=""76""/>。<br/>图（c）弹簧为并联，等效弹簧刚度为3k，则系统的固有频率为：<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5e9b209b-5485-4f70-9209-04e029254009.jpg"" width=""70""/>。由于ω<sub>b</sub>最小，故图（b）装置振动周期最大。"	
"20. 如图4-3-18所示，一弹簧质量系统，置于光滑的斜面上，斜面的倾角α可以在0～90°间改变，则随α的增大系统振动的固有频率{{c1::（）}}。[2009年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""176"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f25c79d0-5609-4f9d-b73c-7b1f8183cdd2.png"" width=""262""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-18</span>"	增大<br>减小<br>不变<br>不能确定	C	系统振动的固有频率只与自身固有的m和k有关，与倾角α无关。	
"21. <p>如图4-3-21所示，质量为m，半径为r的定滑轮O上绕有细绳。依靠摩擦使绳在轮上不打滑，并带动滑轮转动。绳之两端均系质量m的物块A与B。块B放置的光滑斜面倾角为α，0＜α＜π/2，假设定滑轮O的轴承光滑，当系统在两物块的重力作用下运动时，B与O间，A与O间的绳力F<sub>T1</sub>和F<sub>T2</sub>的大小有{{c1::（）}}关系。</p><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""146"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/70dd7ab3-dbe9-43c9-8904-b53d2267ad58.jpg"" width=""202""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-21</span>"	F<sub>T1</sub>=F<sub>T2</sub><br>F<sub>T1</sub>＜F<sub>T2</sub><br>F<sub>T1</sub>＞F<sub>T2</sub><br>只依据已知条件则不能确定	B	"<span style=""font-size:16px;"">在重力作用下，A的加速度方向向下，B的加速度方向沿斜面向上，对定滑轮的受力进行分析，</span><img border=""0"" height=""40"" hspace=""0"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-11-26/d2ee6bae-550c-4ada-8bd6-280f28f35dfe.jpg"" style=""width:294px;height:40px;float:none;"" title=""1.jpg"" vspace=""0"" width=""294""/>，<span style=""font-size:16px;"">其中，<img border=""0"" height=""30"" hspace=""0"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-11-26/a8a1bc39-b34e-44cf-8ed2-9f4e9428e4eb.jpg"" style=""float:none;width:76px;height:30px;"" title=""2.jpg"" vspace=""0"" width=""76""/>，可知<img border=""0"" height=""40"" hspace=""0"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-11-26/2e08f81c-f77d-46de-8a84-07c253f42560.jpg"" style=""width:107px;height:40px;float:none;"" title=""7.jpg"" vspace=""0"" width=""107""/>。</span>"	
"22. 如图4-3-20所示，两个半径和质量相同的均质圆盘A、B放在光滑水平面上，分别受到F<sub>A</sub>、F<sub>B</sub>的作用，如图所示，如F<sub>A</sub>＝F<sub>B</sub>，但在盘上作用的位置不同，则此两圆盘在任一瞬时的质心加速度<img height=""23"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c1525a50-79b1-4d95-b1ea-60a91115ce3d.jpg"" width=""63""/>的关系为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""189"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d88ddf30-56fb-4fdf-8cba-eb488abc9303.jpg"" width=""375""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-20</span>"	"<img height=""23"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5f826c17-e788-4d78-83bb-2a3916fa9c30.jpg"" width=""63""/>异向等值<br><img height=""23"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5f826c17-e788-4d78-83bb-2a3916fa9c30.jpg"" width=""63""/>同向等值<br><img height=""23"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5f826c17-e788-4d78-83bb-2a3916fa9c30.jpg"" width=""63""/>同向，但<img height=""20"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/665dd651-0b6b-4b0b-857a-98b705302a61.jpg"" width=""66""/><br><img height=""23"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5f826c17-e788-4d78-83bb-2a3916fa9c30.jpg"" width=""63""/>同向，但<img height=""20"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/216bb3ca-cca8-4659-9565-a9904915a262.jpg"" width=""66""/>"	B	质心加速度仅与作用在结构上的合外力大小和方向有关，与作用点位置无关，由于两盘受到相同大小与方向的集中力作用，因此它们的质心加速度同向等值。作用点位置不同，则圆盘的角加速度不同。	
"23. 如图4-3-21所示，绳子跨过滑轮O，A端挂重P的人，B端挂着重为P的物块，轮重不计。系统开始时静止，当此人相对绳子以速度u沿绳向上爬时，物块B和人A相对地面的速度应为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""285"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8e6c77bc-8e3e-4b49-b8bf-16814bb5ccc5.jpg"" width=""183""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-21</span>"	"<img height=""23"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/423a3758-cbec-41ba-8a86-bac05f536b12.png"" width=""115""/><br><img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8d3b7272-cce9-4327-86fa-841b7ec015fc.png"" width=""122""/><br><img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/64ead5a6-c463-4186-ad37-7b6cb2c8a978.png"" width=""133""/><br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bc51f512-f25e-405a-987a-74cf56915be2.png"" width=""121""/>"	C	"由于绳的两端拉力均为P，所以系统对O轴的动量矩守恒为：<img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1e45d09a-a0a8-49b0-9f33-18baa60920a2.jpg"" width=""350""/>，又A、B位于绳的两头，速度相等且v<sub>A</sub>+v<sub>B</sub>=u，所以<img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6239962d-9119-439b-a819-6c507b9bd3cf.jpg"" width=""91""/>。"	
"24. 如图4-3-22所示，重为P的小球系于细绳的一端，绳的另一端穿过光滑水平面上的小孔O，令小球在此水平面上沿半径为r的圆周作匀速运动，其速度为v0。如果将绳下拉，使圆周的半径减小为<img height=""38"" id=""图片 1317"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0f6d8df7-c868-4b3b-99a6-8932df5cb4a9.jpg"" width=""19""/>，则此时绳的拉力为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""212"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6e402c40-2c16-4ab1-bb36-786c5aec2063.jpg"" width=""317""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-22</span>"	"<img height=""43"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a11b4203-209a-4a80-ac43-589bd62f94b8.png"" width=""65""/><br><img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b62715a5-7209-4d51-986d-424dd1b9c8c9.png"" width=""64""/><br><img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/25ae2f9e-27c4-4624-8ea3-1e50e814474e.png"" width=""51""/><br><img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a5c67248-138c-4d43-9afa-389a828f650d.png"" width=""65""/>"	B	"小球关于转动中心O的动量矩守恒，即<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b48462c4-2793-46fd-85f2-66e8945e484c.jpg"" width=""103""/>，由此可得v=2v<sub>0</sub> 。于是小球的法向加速度<img height=""58"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/dc8edae5-4c00-42a4-bc20-ade58ca09a4f.jpg"" width=""95""/>，则绳的拉力为<img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/426bf14e-43ce-44de-8804-1f012b5f602a.jpg"" width=""104""/>。"	
"25. 如图4-3-23所示，均质圆轮重W，半径为r，对转轴的回转半径为ρ，以角速度ωO绕水平轴O转动。今用闸杆制动，动摩擦系数μ是常数，轴承摩擦略去不计。要求在t秒钟内停止，则所加铅垂力P为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""250"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e82fc1a8-961f-4073-891a-f14756b78a25.jpg"" width=""385""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-23</span>"	"<img height=""44"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7868adf0-6171-4ad0-9b1e-4cd567376c37.png"" width=""82""/><br><img height=""43"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c027a9c2-57fa-47eb-9c4d-df58ced5d2be.png"" width=""75""/><br><img height=""44"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e95a62d3-d544-4943-b057-eff368f41abe.png"" width=""83""/><br><img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5f2ccb61-5f75-4d60-a0a1-f1cc32baa7e8.png"" width=""62""/>"	A	"根据题意可知，转轴的角加速度大小为<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7614701b-3dce-49ca-88a1-5aabcbb56107.jpg"" width=""52""/>。假设闸杆对转轴的摩擦力为F，建立运动方程得Fr=Jα，即<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1aaa5ef8-61a7-4c17-b6ce-6a7e1ad0e2e7.jpg"" width=""146""/>。由闸杆受力可知闸杆对转轴的压力<img height=""32"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bb42b439-6c0c-410a-9bc1-bfac31497d0a.png"" width=""52""/>于是<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0590292b-87a2-4046-8c68-b47266c2da70.jpg"" width=""196""/>，由此得到<img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e0aecb51-e492-48e2-8c96-a100398f1efb.jpg"" width=""80""/>。"	
"26. 如图4-3-24所示，圆心角为60°的钢制圆弧AB，质量为m，半径为R，质心C距圆心O的距离为<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/08ce2379-5082-45bf-9682-a28898411f56.png"" width=""58""/>则圆弧AB对质心C的转动惯量为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""143"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d148b79b-139e-423d-82a1-b3af6ca77344.jpg"" width=""187""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-24</span>"	"<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/30d46d3c-d501-4388-9001-39710c707d2b.png"" width=""113""/><br><img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f57bb357-a738-4023-9a69-0a913b787bf7.png"" width=""112""/><br><img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a663e52e-5b29-44a7-a266-3f29541463f9.png"" width=""128""/><br><img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bb242373-ef07-4cc7-987c-120fb66456ce.png"" width=""128""/>"	A	"根据平行轴定理，物体对两个平行轴的转动惯量有关系式<img height=""27"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/9810cf59-545e-4b59-b7d7-a75034767473.jpg"" width=""118""/>。因此，圆弧AB对质心C的转动惯量<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2016-12-19/0c1c8a91-7c83-49a3-a8ed-6ee4ef9b93a3.jpg"" title=""2.jpg""/>。"	
"27. 均质等厚零件，如图4-3-25所示，设单位面积的质量为ρ，大圆半径为R，挖去的小圆半径为r，两圆心的距离为a，则零件对过O点并垂直于零件平面的轴的转动惯量为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""275"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bfd5834d-3069-45e7-b6a5-1a8b0fc66d4a.jpg"" width=""289""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-25</span>"	"<img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4ba75326-e16f-496a-bbce-820fe03970e3.png"" width=""191""/><br><img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ba95c7ed-b0bf-4850-8345-e68eadd2f51e.png"" width=""191""/><br><img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a84115d5-d002-4fd2-86d8-3dc159ec4b80.png"" width=""190""/><br><img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/33d429ad-728c-47a7-aafc-8bceb3eabde4.png"" width=""189""/>"	D	"根据题中所给的条件，可得半径为R的大圆对O轴的转动惯量为：<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e2c0cf77-fe14-49c1-bb81-1f953a2fa590.jpg"" width=""179""/><br/>由平行移轴定理可知，半径为r的小圆对O轴的转动惯量为：<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0c49f4eb-7f1a-46e4-9778-a46e5f6415e4.jpg"" width=""335""/><br/>由叠加法可得，零件对O轴的转动惯量为：<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/114dd3b3-0a56-4bd8-a6f8-0b343e16431b.jpg"" width=""258""/>"	
"28. 如图4-3-26所示，忽略质量的细杆OC=l，其端部固结匀质圆盘。杆上点C为圆盘圆心，盘质量为m，半径为r，系统以角速度ω绕轴O转动。系统的动能是{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""201"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/098c47c7-dce1-47f5-a291-7449fccd9a56.jpg"" width=""183""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-26</span>"	"<img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/23b97bc3-9c8d-42c9-9590-6f6d992fd207.png"" width=""97""/><br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f01f0f3c-7bbd-4742-85c4-f6099cfcebb0.png"" width=""135""/><br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/289aa0f9-42e5-47ae-95cb-97585c2fab6e.png"" width=""117""/><br><img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/54598273-67cf-4194-8c89-0c336bd1c0a5.png"" width=""158""/>"	D	"系统中研究对象是细杆和圆盘，又忽略细杆质量，故只需研究圆盘，圆盘整体绕轴O作定轴转动，其动能为<img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5d603461-1966-47cb-b13b-59d0ebd0f091.jpg"" width=""75""/>，且<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5068fe6e-678c-46b5-be9a-3167e3f8ff2a.jpg"" width=""122""/>。"	
"29. 在重量为P的均质圆柱体的中心O处铰接一重量也为P的直杆OA，此直杆的另一端A靠在斜面上，如图4-3-27所示，今使圆柱体做纯滚动，若某瞬时O点速度为v，则此瞬时系统的动能为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""184"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4fe98574-8fc9-419f-a6e3-fb3b6cd2f41e.jpg"" width=""302""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-27</span>"	"<img height=""44"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1e07a81e-5b56-4ca9-89cd-0ecdfadd2b2b.png"" width=""35""/><br><img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ab8373e8-6622-4efc-aae8-b0dd3b9d6419.png"" width=""36""/><br><img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/cd4f94b7-e725-48ea-91d1-e9d22d53387b.png"" width=""28""/><br><img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ec207bd3-4ade-40a1-96e9-7f3dea0be862.png"" width=""33""/>"	A	"杆的动能为<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bba54480-1256-4512-bd5b-cb334c353719.jpg"" width=""56""/>，圆柱的动能为<img height=""44"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/9c76c63a-5141-4457-b8a7-d56bea3f5723.jpg"" width=""194""/>，因此，系统的动能为<img height=""44"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ac5017d3-0dc7-4c38-90d2-b228b98cbb73.jpg"" width=""127""/>。"	
"30. 一质量弹簧系统铅垂悬挂如图4-3-28所示，若取系统静平衡位置为零势能位置，物体各自离开静平衡位置的位移为x<sub>1</sub>和x<sub>2</sub>，则系统总势能为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""349"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e502e3ae-4276-4ce6-bd4b-59a76aed7cbf.jpg"" width=""184""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-28</span>"	"<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/81ffc9cf-8665-473c-9ce2-eb6fcd4e5909.png"" width=""239""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0f6ac832-c31a-4025-b93e-21bb1dbeac23.png"" width=""175""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4ca89ed1-ece0-40db-864d-94ba897dd6b7.png"" width=""340""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/90fe5bfc-dc34-4cbc-be1b-ebd47b36753d.png"" width=""113""/>"	B	"静平衡位置为零势能位置，图中位置并非静平衡位置。总重力势能增量为-m<sub>1</sub>gx<sub>1</sub>-m<sub>2</sub>gx<sub>2</sub>，总弹簧势能增量为：<img height=""45"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/af562543-91d9-4ea5-9f07-f64833796e7c.jpg"" width=""576""/><br/>则系统总势能为：<img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d988b13f-0ef7-4ef7-a0ba-7c66d910394a.jpg"" width=""183""/>。"	
"31. 如图4-3-29所示，半径为R，质量为m的均质圆盘由铰支座和绳约束，铰O与质心C位于水平位置。当剪断绳的瞬时，圆盘的ω<sub>O</sub>和α<sub>O</sub>分别为______；当OC转至与水平成90°时圆盘的ω和α分别为______。{{c1::（）}}<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""240"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/71b50326-e125-4110-9848-9e226e77bc7e.jpg"" width=""246""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-29</span>"	"<img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/dfbcf441-f8e6-4c9f-942c-31aed84d28d2.png"" width=""259""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/97520226-f6cc-425b-9e9d-ed45748344ae.png"" width=""244""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bf4aff66-150e-4550-8e8d-50bcbc41c231.png"" width=""246""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c5cb495b-1dee-44a9-a356-26e3d9956349.png"" width=""255""/>"	B	"绳被剪断瞬间，圆盘尚未开始旋转，角速度ω<sub>O</sub>=0；虽然圆盘速度为零，但由于受到重力作用，圆盘有旋转的趋势，因此，角加速度不等于零，由Jα=Fr，即<img height=""38"" id=""图片 1372"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/23cd10d5-a0a2-469a-997c-0e824d9e7170.jpg"" width=""115""/>，可得<img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7b7826b2-fe3b-4870-a306-8723463d44e4.jpg"" width=""55""/>；当OC转至与水平成90°即铅垂位置时，根据机械能守恒，OC处于水平位置时的机械能等于OC处于铅垂位置时的机械能，于是有<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/943668e6-9949-436e-901d-755eb7fdcf8c.jpg"" width=""93""/>，可得<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1a630bc7-bbd0-4804-9017-7fed78abc01f.jpg"" width=""65""/>；而当OC转至铅垂位置时，圆盘在水平方向上不受力，因此加速度为零，角加速度也为零。"	
"32. 如图4-3-30所示，均质杆OA长为l，质量为m，以角速度ω及角加速度α绕O轴转动，则惯性力系的简化结果为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""78"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7800c326-57f2-4305-b9f1-4f34400fb21a.jpg"" width=""356""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-30</span>"	"<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4670b40b-8b6f-426c-8991-967acd1f226a.png"" width=""269""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/98765c25-7d8e-45a4-b157-5e676367039b.png"" width=""266""/><br><img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a463f9aa-ca2b-49ca-90f1-7ddbf51052af.png"" width=""282""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/39b5d7ed-cd8b-4b48-8158-75de0b8c74ac.png"" width=""281""/>"	B	"刚体绕定轴转动时，惯性力系向转轴简化得一惯性力和一惯性力偶。惯性力大小等于刚体质量与质心加速度的乘积，方向与质心加速度方向相反，作用线通过转轴，故<img height=""28"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e09667c9-4948-4c42-b16b-d3fc8c2d5f17.jpg"" width=""85""/>，作用于O点；惯性力偶的力偶矩等于刚体对转轴的转动惯量与角加速度的乘积，转向与角加速度相反，即<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1c7ebd6f-c6a8-463e-887f-9467a7ac76e1.jpg"" width=""173""/>。"	
"33. 均质细杆AB长L，重力的大小为P，与铅垂轴固结成角α＝30°，并以匀角速度ω转动，如图4-3-31所示。则惯性力系的合力的大小等于{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""301"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b62ce68f-b0c3-4892-b4b7-9458479d5867.jpg"" width=""139""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-31</span>"	"<img height=""24"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/017e182d-181b-4fa4-8400-2788d8157073.png"" width=""86""/><br><img height=""24"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8334dd0c-95bb-4cb5-90a4-fc449c88a3c4.png"" width=""70""/><br><img height=""22"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/853f665f-f3aa-4ef6-8b43-768812d2ceec.png"" width=""64""/><br><img height=""24"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/639ebeb0-63d9-4ec6-8b02-a3f8603af333.png"" width=""65""/>"	D	"均质杆AB的质心C的加速度为<img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/9c36c83c-f466-405b-8810-49d755c6610a.jpg"" width=""213""/>，因此惯性力的合力<img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5e905af7-db57-4bed-be25-599569b6921c.jpg"" width=""116""/>。"	
"34. 如图4-3-32所示，均质圆轮质量为m，轮上绕以细绳，绳的一端固定不动。轮心从初始位置A0无初速度下落。则当轮心降落高度为h时绳子一端的拉力T为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""260"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b6a26f55-2fa7-4e1e-849e-fd1dbc77dc76.jpg"" width=""215""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-32</span>"	"<img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b9b79cf8-6776-4213-9e61-3a0e843b1972.png"" width=""63""/><br><img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c2cc9df7-bc20-4c3b-9f44-7ffc8eb26083.png"" width=""65""/><br><img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/13ea7363-9771-489b-8f7e-b0b9f5df5235.png"" width=""63""/><br><img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/2c3a9fd0-a4f3-465d-b67f-6da8c159dbdc.png"" width=""61""/>"	B	"利用达朗贝尔原理，并将惯性力向质心简化，（mg-ma<sub>c</sub>）与T形成力偶矩使圆轮转动，转动力矩为M：<img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d7773f33-e412-477e-ab43-7fa43e3ef0c8.jpg"" width=""249""/>，由此得到<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8e39ef09-5d5b-4dff-9fdd-1c3e4448b5b6.jpg"" width=""246""/>。"	
"35. 汽车重W，以匀加速度a沿水平直线道路向右运动，其重心C离地面的高度为h，汽车的前、后轴到通过其重心C的垂线的距离分别为L1和L2，如图4-3-33所示。地面对汽车前轮的正压力N1与对后轮的正压力N2的大小分别为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""164"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8f5e66cd-6332-4e71-8c49-e3dc3f3d8882.jpg"" width=""361""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-33</span>"	"<img height=""43"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f61b0e5d-18a0-4092-8f5f-fa7cd2e4497c.png"" width=""267""/><br><img height=""43"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/981ba07d-e9f1-4482-9720-55a1352ea16a.png"" width=""262""/><br><img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5b77f996-ecab-4795-b80a-dd0eb69d5e6d.png"" width=""263""/><br><img height=""45"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/79a0b1ab-727d-4a40-811d-9189978c3483.png"" width=""264""/>"	C	"根据达朗贝尔原理，惯性力<img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/81579c2a-33ee-458c-b8ba-1754763254c6.jpg"" width=""125""/>，则：<br/>①对后轮取矩，N<sub>1</sub>（L<sub>1</sub>+L<sub>2</sub>）=WL<sub>2</sub>-Fh，则<img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/056c217b-4b0a-4002-87bf-63d6a7ba7d93.jpg"" width=""123""/>；<br/>②对前轮取矩，N<sub>2</sub>（L<sub>1</sub>+L<sub>2</sub>）=WL<sub>1</sub>+Fh，则<img height=""51"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a56dd4d2-69c1-4559-a8ea-0733b22cd29e.jpg"" width=""123""/>。"	
"36. 如图4-3-34所示，弹簧—物块直线振动系统中，物块质量m，两根弹簧的刚度系数各为k<sub>1</sub>与k<sub>2</sub>，若用一根等效弹簧代替这两根弹簧，则其刚度系数k为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""71"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/406f49b3-3e3b-45f8-a747-f73e234be66a.jpg"" width=""290""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-34</span>"	"<img height=""47"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4e287a4c-a45d-420d-874a-f4d9e79f0c15.png"" width=""82""/><br><img height=""50"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6ef84861-545e-43ca-b7e6-e79f001c1725.png"" width=""82""/><br><img height=""46"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/69253848-0f99-4fcb-8a99-20a2f4a95dba.png"" width=""84""/><br><img height=""28"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/31683a08-3ddb-4103-825e-084b53f6d35c.png"" width=""86""/>"	D	等效弹簧在振动中发生的形变与原弹簧的形变量相等，假定原弹簧振动中收缩（或伸长量）为l，则由mk<sub>1</sub>l+mk<sub>2</sub>l=mkl，得k=k<sub>1</sub>+k<sub>2</sub>（或由k<sub>1</sub>、k<sub>2</sub>并联直接得出）。	
"37. 如图4-3-35所示，弹簧—物块直线振动系统位于铅垂面内。弹簧刚度系数为k，物块质量为m。若已知物块的运动微分方程为<img height=""19"" id=""图片 1407"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6e1cdac3-7aa5-4b33-a49f-e8f9ec40350d.jpg"" width=""29""/>+kx=0，则描述运动的坐标O<sub>x</sub>的坐标原点应为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""228"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d963f427-a000-46f8-a2a4-188bbf7667ba.jpg"" width=""141""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图4-3-35</span>"	弹簧悬挂处之点O<sub>1</sub><br>弹簧原长l0处之点O<sub>2</sub><br>弹簧由物块重力引起静伸长δ<sub>st</sub>处之点O<sub>3</sub><br>任意点皆可	C	由方程mx．．+kx=0可知，当x=0时，加速度为0，在点O<sub>3</sub>处符合。	
"1. 弯截面杆，轴向受力如图5-1-1所示，杆的最大轴力是{{c1::（）}}kN。[2010年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""92"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/88bd47bb-82d8-4631-ae75-1aef715c8319.jpg"" width=""348""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-1</span>"	8<br>5<br>3<br>12	B	由截面法可得，杆件所受轴力从左端起，依次为：F<sub>N1</sub>=-3kN，F<sub>N2</sub>=5kN，故杆的最大轴力为5kN。	
"2. 图5-1-2所示结构的两杆面积和材料相同，在铅直向下的力F作用下，下面正确的结论是{{c1::（）}}。[2014年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""243"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/18ebab0f-5722-4e0e-92df-efed9ac66e62.png"" width=""186""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-2</span>"	C点位移向下偏左，1杆轴力不为零<br>C点位移向下偏左，1杆轴力为零<br>C点位移铅直向下，1杆轴力为零<br>C点位移向下偏右，1杆轴力不为零	B	"首先取节点C为研究对象，根据节点C的平衡可知，杆1受力为零，杆2的轴力为拉力F；再考虑两杆的变形，杆1无变形，杆2受拉伸长。由于变形后两根杆仍然要连在一起，因此C点变形后的位置，应该在以A点为圆心，以杆1原长为半径的圆弧，和以B点为圆心、以伸长后的杆2长度为半径的圆弧的交点C′上，如图5-1-3所示。显然这个点在C点向下偏左的位置。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""244"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/eb13112d-68ea-4e31-80d0-0faf2bad6868.png"" width=""169""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-3</span>"	
"3. 图5-1-4所示结构的两杆面积和材料相同，在铅直力F作用下，拉伸正应力最先达到许用应力的杆是{{c1::（）}}。[2013年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""175"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1a6be530-e30f-4576-8a2a-092884d7e021.png"" width=""192""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-4</span>"	杆1<br>杆2<br>同时达到<br>不能确定	B	"对C点进行受力分析，∑F<sub>x</sub>=0，F<sub>2</sub>sin30°-F<sub>1</sub>sin45°=0，∑F<sub>y</sub>=0，F<sub>1</sub>cos45°+F<sub>2</sub>cos30°-F=0，得<img height=""39"" id=""图片 1"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8e04a3f7-b148-4265-b3ac-0322584cb762.jpg"" width=""197""/>，F<sub>2</sub>＞F<sub>1</sub>。又两杆面积和材料相同，由正应力公式<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/505665f1-e2b4-4666-beda-a0aaeca8882a.jpg"" width=""54""/>可得σ<sub>2</sub>＞σ<sub>1</sub>，故杆2先达到许用应力。"	
"4. 图5-1-5所示结构的两杆许用应力均为［σ］，杆1的面积为A，杆2的面积为2A，则该结构的许用载荷是{{c1::（）}}。[2013年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""183"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/098145d8-ad62-4b74-8403-77a43758750e.png"" width=""176""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-5</span>"	［F］=A［σ］<br>［F］=2A［σ］<br>［F］=3A［σ］<br>［F］=4A［σ］	B	"杆1和杆2的的轴力分别为<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/63e9d42b-a272-492d-9168-926051439812.jpg"" width=""219""/>且<img height=""30"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/707a4959-ed83-4610-8dac-295ad18586f2.jpg"" width=""81""/>，取较小值，故［F］=2A［σ］。"	
"5. 圆截面杆ABC轴向受力如图5-1-6，已知BC杆的直径d=100mm，AB杆的直径为2d，杆的最大的拉应力是{{c1::（）}}。[2014、2011年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""113"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/84488ea0-6058-4823-adb2-c463848659c9.png"" width=""342""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-6</span>"	40MPa<br>30MPa<br>80MPa<br>120MPa	A	"杆AB和杆BC的的轴力分别为<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-02-16/a982dc27-591e-4969-8101-579dbbd53229.jpg"" title=""1.jpg""/>。根据<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-02-16/4acfa617-2966-4c2d-99fc-fef55e36b92a.jpg"" title=""2.jpg""/>解得：<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-02-16/31c32a12-c62b-46f1-a9ff-467a3bab3baa.jpg"" title=""3.jpg""/>，<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-02-16/0d421437-9293-4ff1-b65f-59b0cd327c5b.jpg"" title=""4.jpg""/>，各杆应力不变，故其最大拉应力经计算为BC杆截面处40MPa。"	
6. 桁架由2根细长直杆组成，杆的截面尺寸相同，材料分别是结构钢和普通铸铁。下列桁架中，布局比较合理的是{{c1::（）}}。[2014年真题]	"<img height=""112"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/47ecab30-a54e-4e8f-ab69-74d435d34ff7.png"" width=""176""/><br><img height=""116"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a8198a9c-0fc2-4708-9047-276752c6ae80.png"" width=""172""/><br><img height=""112"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f0d7299a-4664-4f30-a960-5fc3dfda6b82.png"" width=""186""/><br><img height=""114"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/246b0b1e-74fa-4680-b2bf-82d6e99a53d2.png"" width=""182""/>"	D	由于钢的抗拉性能较好而抗压性能较差，铸铁抗拉强度较差而抗压强度较好，故铸铁受压力时布局较为合适。对上述四种布局进行受力分析，只有AD两项符合要求，其布局中均是钢承受拉力而铸铁承受压力；而对于受压的构件，长细比不宜过大，故铸铁的构件长度应较短些，即只有D项布局比较合理。	
7. 截面面积为A的等截面直杆，受轴向拉力作用。杆件的原始材料为低碳钢，若将材料改为木材，其他条件不变，下列结论中正确的是{{c1::（）}}。[2012年真题]	正应力增大，轴向变形增大<br>正应力减小，轴向变形减小<br>正应力不变，轴向变形增大<br>正应力减小，轴向变形不变	C	"根据公式<img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ca0ebbfa-408e-41bb-b560-a5e485496a34.jpg"" width=""48""/>，由于FN和A都不变，故正应力不变。根据公式<img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ed252407-b193-486e-8f90-812ba09eab35.jpg"" width=""67""/>，由于木材的弹性模量减小，故轴向变形ΔL增大。"	
"8. 图5-1-7所示拉杆承受轴向拉力P的作用，设斜截面m—m的面积为A，则σ=P/A为{{c1::（）}}。[2008年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""65"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/01220aab-2f0a-4ae8-ac5d-55f2a64fe968.jpg"" width=""261""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-7</span>"	横截面上的正应力<br>斜截面上的正应力<br>斜截面上的应力<br>斜截面上的剪应力	C	"横截面拉伸正应力：σ=P/S，S为正截面面积；记斜截面m—m的法线与x轴夹角为α，则斜截面上的正应力和切应力为：<img height=""64"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ecec0a80-d2ba-4f54-aacd-84cfcdd9e5e3.jpg"" width=""165""/>而Pα=P/A为斜截面上的正应力和切应力的合力即斜截面上的应力。"	
"9. 图5-1-8所示等截面直杆，材料的抗压刚度为EA，杆中距离A端1.5L处横截面的轴向位移是{{c1::（）}}。[2012年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""101"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/fb1c1e45-f330-4a51-8a44-8879fc326bca.png"" width=""366""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-8</span>"	"<img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/54594a4a-01df-4cc3-811b-150a99d31a3e.png"" width=""25""/><br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/81790697-068b-4b0d-b096-c1aafe950888.png"" width=""27""/><br><img height=""34"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/9b511255-6133-4b41-8adf-14e26e800e30.png"" width=""24""/><br><img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/728b7b7b-9920-4b80-8746-6ef7175a8449.png"" width=""22""/>"	D	"根据求轴力的直接法可得AB段轴力F<sub>N1</sub>=F，BC段轴力F<sub>N</sub>2=0，CD段轴力FN3=2F。分析可知所求横截面的轴向位移就等于AB段的伸长量<img height=""32"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/17d31341-e356-4d41-ac62-28095aad165e.jpg"" width=""55""/>。"	
10. 两拉杆的材料和所受拉力都相同，且均处在弹性范围内，若两杆长度相等，横截面面积A<sub>1</sub>＞A<sub>2</sub>，则{{c1::（）}}。[2008年真题]	Δl<sub>1</sub>＜Δl<sub>2</sub>；ε<sub>1</sub>=ε<sub>2</sub><br>Δl<sub>1</sub>=Δl<sub>2</sub>；ε1＜ε<sub>2</sub><br>Δl<sub>1</sub>＜Δl<sub>2</sub>；ε1＜ε<sub>2</sub><br>Δl<sub>1</sub>=Δl<sub>2</sub>；ε1=ε<sub>2</sub>	C	"纵向变形的胡克定律：<img height=""32"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/837e1535-6faa-4478-801f-baaf356d2b98.jpg"" width=""50""/>；纵向线应变：<img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/27a12922-e46c-44fc-9d9d-551b737b2830.jpg"" width=""43""/>。在比例极限内，杆的纵向变形Δl与轴力N、杆长l成正比，与乘积EA成反比。故Δl<sub>1</sub>＜Δl<sub>2</sub>，ε<sub>1</sub>＜ε<sub>2</sub>。"	
"11. 等直杆的受力情况如图5-1-9所示，则杆内最大轴力Nmax和最小轴力Nmin分别为{{c1::（）}}。[2007年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""77"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/12452750-ef48-4eb0-94c5-97bc2fe68358.jpg"" width=""426""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-9</span>"	N<sub>max</sub>=60kN；N<sub>min</sub>=15kN<br>N<sub>max</sub>=60kN；N<sub>min</sub>=15kN<br>N<sub>max</sub>=30kN；N<sub>min</sub>=-30kN<br>N<sub>max</sub>=90kN；N<sub>min</sub>=-60kN	C	"作直杆的轴力图，如图5-1-10所示，则N<sub>max</sub>=30kN；N<sub>min</sub>=-30kN。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""90"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1b2029b1-814a-48cf-b218-0d98740dcb28.jpg"" width=""392""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-10</span>"	
12. 横截面面积为A的等截面直杆受力F作用发生轴向拉伸变形，其30°斜截面上的正应力和切应力分别为{{c1::（）}}。	"<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7d4bf289-0060-4ae2-85e4-0e0d0199fbbd.png"" width=""60""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/be35e2da-a063-4d4d-8604-7554f8ab2b5d.png"" width=""60""/><br><img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7ff620cf-6fda-48ef-91e8-4849291a577c.png"" width=""59""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7b030919-63c2-404f-adb8-bfe6b4f094d0.png"" width=""62""/>"	D	"横截面上的正应力为：<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/31a56b40-b742-4e1e-b2af-3f91f921786b.png"" width=""56""/>30°斜截面正应力为：<img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/015d667b-55d7-44b9-b152-34f49a51fa60.png"" width=""176""/>切应力为：<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0fedc90b-3719-4ba0-b136-d5d060713a1b.jpg"" width=""196""/>。"	
"13. 如图5-1-11所示结构中，杆①、②、③的轴力分别为：N<sub>1</sub>、N<sub>2</sub>、N<sub>3</sub>，轴向线应变分别为：ε<sub>1</sub>、ε<sub>2</sub>、ε<sub>3</sub>。已知三根水平杆的EA相同，忽略梁AB的变形，则三杆轴力及线应变的关系为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""258"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/2d109d01-2074-463d-bd57-06467c00ce55.jpg"" width=""271""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-11</span>"	N<sub>1</sub>＝N<sub>2</sub>＝N<sub>3</sub>，ε<sub>1</sub>＜ε<sub>2</sub>＜ε<sub>3</sub><br>N<sub>1</sub><N<sub>2</sub><N<sub>3</sub>，ε<sub>1</sub>＜ε<sub>2</sub>＜ε<sub>3</sub><br>N<sub>1</sub>＝N<sub>2</sub>＝N<sub>3</sub>，ε<sub>1</sub>＝ε<sub>2</sub>＝ε<sub>3</sub><br>N<sub>1</sub>＜N<sub>2</sub>＜N<sub>3</sub>，ε<sub>1</sub>＝ε<sub>2</sub>＝ε<sub>3</sub>	C	"由几何变形协调条件Δl<sub>1</sub>∶Δl<sub>2</sub>∶Δl<sub>3</sub>＝1∶2∶3和物理方程<img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8535b3dc-8b53-4128-a252-fbf487a32139.jpg"" width=""265""/>，可知：N<sub>1</sub>＝N<sub>2</sub>＝N3；再根据胡克定律<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c5d4cb99-65ae-4839-9b6e-82c333abceb0.jpg"" width=""86""/>，可得：ε<sub>1</sub>＝ε<sub>2</sub>＝ε<sub>3</sub>。"	
"14. 某装配组件的尺寸与受力如图5-1-12所示，已知垂直杆ABC的AB段与BC段材料相同，横截面面积分别为A<sub>1</sub>、A2<sub>，</sub>若载荷P<sub>1</sub>、P<sub>2</sub>作用下C点的垂直位移为零，则P<sub>2</sub>与P<sub>1</sub>之间的关系为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""254"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6d71fd0a-73b1-4af3-9718-4733f4d14778.jpg"" width=""290""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-12</span>"	"<img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/af80c5ea-0dab-4d69-9a24-a0942e803091.png"" width=""110""/><br><img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7e17bec5-61c9-4cac-9772-1c5acecdd0f7.png"" width=""111""/><br><img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/eeb04535-3595-4ae5-ae81-ac50bbb8faaf.png"" width=""109""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/44caefee-3fc1-445f-ba6a-a2215b84feb1.png"" width=""109""/>"	C	"由题可知，C点的垂直位移为零，即AB段的缩短量与BC段的伸长量相等，<br/>建立方程得：<img border=""0"" height=""40"" hspace=""0"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-06-17/61d901c2-fca9-4dc2-97fc-d942a0b92db6.jpg"" style=""width:73px;height:40px;float:none;"" title=""1.jpg"" vspace=""0"" width=""73""/><br/>其中杆的轴力为：<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-06-17/815815cf-5667-4c5c-ba17-ff6391bd1949.jpg"" title=""2.jpg""/><span style=""font-size:14px"">（压力），<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-06-17/f1362e48-593a-4afe-998c-484a834d85a9.jpg"" title=""3.jpg""/></span><span style=""font-size:14px"">（拉力）</span><br/>由此可求得：<img border=""0"" height=""45"" hspace=""0"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2017-06-17/9d9adfa3-a29a-48c1-988c-a314621f2104.jpg"" style=""width:127px;height:45px;float:none;"" title=""4.jpg"" vspace=""0"" width=""127""/>"	
"15. 图5-1-13所示刚梁AB由杆1和杆2支承。已知两杆的材料相同，长度不等，横截面面积分别为A<sub>1</sub>和A<sub>2</sub>。若荷载P使刚梁平行下移，则A<sub>1</sub>和A<sub>2</sub>关系正确的是{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""220"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/dedc4647-2d8e-49bd-be4c-d1c1dbf7887f.jpg"" width=""182""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-13</span>"	A<sub>1</sub>＜A<sub>2</sub><br>A<sub>1</sub>=A<sub>2</sub><br>A<sub>1</sub>＞A<sub>2</sub><br>A<sub>1</sub>、A<sub>2</sub>为任意	C	"根据<img height=""32"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7ce3da1b-0757-48fb-b88a-d5f08be81b8d.jpg"" width=""51""/>,又1、2杆的轴力相等均为P/2，1、2杆的长度伸长量相同，则<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6ab4cb60-9b5f-4316-af66-d2b42b9f13e0.jpg"" width=""78""/>，已知l<sub>1</sub>＞l<sub>2</sub>，得A<sub>1</sub>＞A<sub>2</sub>。"

"17. 如图5-1-15所示结构中，D点作用竖向荷载P时，杆AB的轴向应变为ε，假设此时杆AB仅发生弹性变形，忽略梁CD的变形，则梁端D的竖向位移为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""171"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/aee527dc-f974-40b0-b27c-4aaa898e7d8a.jpg"" width=""277""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-15</span>"	"εa<br>2εa<br><img height=""19"" id=""图片 1480"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/dd5af042-2618-4d48-940e-256f38317b4d.jpg"" width=""48""/><br>4εa"	D	"根据题中所给条件，可知杆AB的伸长量为：ΔL<sub>AB</sub>＝εL<sub>AB</sub>＝<img height=""22"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/88cebfc3-e0d1-4db2-8c2a-785b8dce569e.jpg"" width=""35""/>。利用垂线代替微圆弧的方法，作如图5-1-16所示变形图，由图得：S＝<img height=""21"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/93979ed8-f872-4cc1-a9a9-ad8871398a2c.jpg"" width=""49""/>＝2εa，则梁端D的竖向位移为2S＝4εa。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""196"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c51def7d-473e-4b87-a835-f4dd1741c88b.jpg"" width=""269""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-1-16</span>"

"1. 钢板用两个铆钉固定在支座上，铆钉直径为d，在图5-2-1所示载荷下，铆钉的最大切应力是{{c1::（）}}。[2013、2010年真题]<br /><span style=""display:block;text-align:center""><strong><img id=""图片 1"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/17cc710f-d0b5-498f-aaf4-bcbe00b808cb.jpg"" /></strong></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-1</span>"	"<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c68e2448-c626-418c-92a7-b4d52f007019.png"" /><br /><img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c77a495f-5d39-481a-80c7-2ee2eb47c35b.png"" /><br /><img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/aefa54b2-8015-48a2-a965-f24189e1bdfc.png"" /><br /><img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7ab80cc3-4eef-456b-be92-1b8f6db1318f.png"" />"	C	"根据题意可知，铆钉组的形心在AB的中点，可以将力F平移至铆钉组的形心，并附加一个<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8dde951c-455c-479f-aa2a-1eabe81b3d98.jpg"" />的顺时针力偶矩。在通过铆钉组截面形心的力F作用下，每个铆钉上所受的力相等，即<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b52da3fe-25a1-462c-836f-83be85dd46cd.jpg"" />。而在力偶矩M<sub>e</sub>的作用下，每个铆钉所受的力与其至铆钉组截面形心的距离r成正比，则F<sub>A2</sub>=F<sub>B2</sub>。由合力矩定理∑F<sub>i2</sub>r<sub>i</sub>=M<sub>e</sub>,得<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/9beb10fe-da82-4fec-8ad3-090a8895c234.jpg"" />,有：<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/dea3a482-188a-4e7b-aee7-52e2948b3e6e.jpg"" />,则铆钉的最大切应力<img src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7809f0c5-5ce8-4e05-9a21-2ca994d2a8e9.jpg"" />。"	
"2. 冲床在钢板上冲一圆孔，如图5-2-2所示，圆孔直径d=100mm，钢板的厚度t=10mm，钢板的剪切强度极限τ<sub>b</sub>=300MPa，需要的冲击力F是{{c1::（）}}。[2014年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""185"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f2ac125a-12d7-467b-a00a-c12106783eb9.jpg"" width=""272""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-2</span>"	F=300πKN<br>F=3000πKN<br>F=2500πKN<br>F=7500πKN	A	本题中，受冲切面积A=πdt，根据公式F=τ<sub>b</sub>A，代入数值得：F=300πkN。	
"3. 图5-2-3所示螺钉承受轴向拉力F，螺钉头与钢板之间的挤压应力是{{c1::（）}}。[2013年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""293"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/22493a31-d705-4d79-a8b4-a5b1fc62d07b.png"" width=""366""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-3</span>"	"<img height=""43"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/036596d9-97b5-4e41-8f27-f19338fcb1ab.png"" width=""134""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/3d472a49-f5f3-4f1e-b1fc-c2c4180503fc.png"" width=""75""/><br><img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1e334f3c-e8a0-42c4-a692-418229a59b71.png"" width=""72""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bdf405cb-5d33-403f-af5c-6b7e24a66969.png"" width=""79""/>"	A	"由题可得，挤压面积<img height=""38"" id=""图片 1518"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b61588eb-4f6d-406e-9d77-2e4ba842e555.jpg"" width=""106""/>，挤压应力<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8dccb62a-155e-46d5-8f9b-c0edf6c1c499.jpg"" width=""169""/>。"	
"4. 图5-2-4所示冲床的冲压力F=300πkN，钢板的厚度t=10mm，钢板的剪切强度极限τ<sub>b</sub>=300MPa。冲床在钢板上可冲圆孔的最大直径d是{{c1::（）}}。[2012年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""201"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/9c239715-8b53-48d1-afcb-9bb2c46ba982.png"" width=""324""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-4</span>"	d=200mm<br>d=100mm<br>d=4000mm<br>d=1000mm	B	"剪切面面积A<sub>S</sub>=πdt，剪力F<sub>S</sub>=F，由剪切强度定义得：<img height=""44"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4c652eae-019f-47ad-8544-594ca7ba1a31.jpg"" width=""105""/>。所以<img height=""45"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/bdd3cfb6-e7f3-4fea-a475-a16d4854a0c9.jpg"" width=""210""/>。"	
"5. 螺钉受力如图5-2-5，已知螺钉和钢板的材料相同，拉伸许用应力[σ]是剪切许用应力[τ]的2倍，即[σ]=2[τ]，钢板厚度t是螺钉高度h的1.5倍，则螺钉直径d的合理值是{{c1::（）}}。[2014年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""233"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/2d2ed1e3-c2fc-4bd4-8825-6dd5b0b3c179.png"" width=""255""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-5</span>"	d=2h<br>d=0.5h<br>d<sup>2</sup>=2Dt<br>d<sup>2</sup>=0.5Dt	A	对螺钉以及钢板进行受力分析可知，螺钉受轴向拉力，螺钉与钢板同时受剪切力。根据F=τA可知，剪切力危险点应出现在受力面小处，故出现在螺钉处。当轴向力等于剪切力时，即F<sub>轴</sub>=σА=σπd<sup>2</sup>/4=τА=τhπd，螺钉直径合理值d=2h。	
"6. 图5-2-6所示两根木杆连接结构，已知木材的许用切应力为［τ］，许用挤压应力为［σ<sub>bs</sub>］，则a与h的合理比值是{{c1::（）}}。[2012年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""157"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/66badfb3-ff7e-42b1-a06b-fedbe029aa5f.png"" width=""402""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-6</span>"	"<img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/cf289b9a-0e7a-4d39-b836-f12a3585f9d3.png"" width=""79""/><br><img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/dbb63807-d7d7-4097-98ce-4034903161ec.png"" width=""78""/><br><img height=""43"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1caaf995-c6cf-4b08-83e4-c1175f534f8e.png"" width=""76""/><br><img height=""42"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/16bde434-4f9c-4fc6-8038-bf130378fa6c.png"" width=""88""/>"	A	"取一根木杆为研究对象，可看出剪切面面积A<sub>s</sub>=ab，挤压面面积A<sub>bs</sub>=hb。由<img height=""46"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0351ce96-9141-4a4b-a0f7-e51b64163322.png"" width=""302""/>。两式相除，可得：<img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/cf289b9a-0e7a-4d39-b836-f12a3585f9d3.png"" width=""79""/>。"	
"7. 已知铆钉的许用切应力为［τ］，许用挤压应力为［σ<sub>bs</sub>］，钢板的厚度为t，则图5-2-7所示铆钉直径d与钢板厚度t的关系是{{c1::（）}}。[2011年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""107"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d5a337cc-f4f7-4a5a-ad6b-5c13d77ec023.jpg"" width=""372""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-6</span>"	"<img height=""43"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/19ca2d73-90ba-41a1-93a7-fbeed278cf86.png"" width=""82""/><br><img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/564492ac-fc37-4179-abab-a84c7150c0e6.png"" width=""83""/><br><img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/579d7565-ea49-4f6c-9211-5abb514a24c1.png"" width=""85""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4ec82e0c-031a-4cb3-a03c-e3d5e50dfe27.png"" width=""81""/>"	B	"由临界条件求得：<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/cb5386c9-114b-4476-bec0-0dbb04fffd0c.jpg"" width=""203""/>。联立上述两式，解得：<img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/564492ac-fc37-4179-abab-a84c7150c0e6.png"" width=""83""/>。"	
"8. 如图5-2-8所示，在平板和受拉螺栓之间垫上一个垫圈，可以提高{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""173"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c083477f-25b3-4e55-b843-75559b48c617.jpg"" width=""199""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-8</span>"	螺栓的拉伸强度<br>螺栓的剪切强度<br>螺栓的挤压强度<br>平板的挤压强度	D	增加垫圈之后，平板所受到的挤压面积由螺栓面积变为垫圈面积，面积增大，从而使其挤压强度提高。	
"9. 如图5-2-9所示，A和B的直径都为d，则两者中最大剪应力为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""190"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d029c0ef-7788-47c2-ae0d-67630a308c0e.jpg"" width=""290""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-9</span>"	4bP/（aπd<sup>2</sup>）<br>4（a+b）P/（aπd<sup>2</sup>）<br>4（a+b）P/（bπd<sup>2</sup>）<br>4aP/（bπd<sup>2</sup>）	B	"由受力分析可知，A、B受到的剪力分别为：<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/02b2335b-b66c-4969-8258-11c37af616a3.jpg"" width=""188""/>，<br/>显然F<sub>SB</sub>>F<sub>SA</sub>，因此：<img height=""78"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7e457043-a063-4ed7-8a69-2600c7eab68f.jpg"" width=""225""/>。"	
"10. 如图5-2-10所示，一截面为正方形的混凝土柱浇筑在双层混凝土基础上，两层混凝土基础的厚度均为t，许用剪应力[τ]＝1.5MPa。已知柱传递的荷载P＝220kN，若地基对混凝土板的反力均匀分布，则不会使基础发生剪切破坏的基础厚度t至少应为{{c1::（）}}mm。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""212"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d0c78664-5110-4ad3-94ab-6c2224d5451c.jpg"" width=""340""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-10</span>"	105<br>111.1<br>166.7<br>172	A	"据题意按上层基础强度条件计算可得：<br/><img height=""83"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b75dbb79-e3a3-4ca0-92ab-5f4c178f3813.jpg"" width=""414""/><br/>按下层基础强度条件计算：<br/><img height=""83"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d7aed257-4d23-48e1-a622-3416f1404de8.jpg"" width=""411""/><br/>所以t至少应为105mm。"	
"11. 四个直径为d的铆钉将托架固定在立柱上，如图5-2-11所示。铆钉间距为a，外力P到立柱中心线的距离为b，如铆钉自上至下的编号为1、2、3、4，对应的铆钉所受的剪力数值为Q<sub>1</sub>、Q<sub>2</sub>、Q<sub>3</sub>、Q<sub>4</sub>，则各剪力之间的关系为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""287"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e8ec8d21-6e1e-4f8f-a6cd-a75a11c9db99.jpg"" width=""226""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-2-11</span>"	Q<sub>1</sub>＝Q<sub>2</sub>＝Q<sub>3</sub>＝Q<sub>4</sub><br>Q<sub>1</sub>＜Q<sub>2</sub>＜Q<sub>3</sub>＜Q<sub>4</sub><br>Q<sub>1</sub>＝Q<sub>4</sub>＞Q<sub>3</sub>＝Q<sub>2</sub><br>Q<sub>1</sub>＝Q<sub>4</sub>＜Q<sub>3</sub>＝Q<sub>2</sub>	C	将集中外力P等效作用到立柱中心线上，可得等效荷载为一大小为P、方向向下的集中荷载和一大小为Pb、沿顺时针方向的力偶矩。根据四个铆钉的位置关系可知，四个铆钉各自承担的竖直向剪力均为P/4；水平向剪力则因各铆钉距离铆钉组形心的距离的不同而不同，1号、4号铆钉与铆钉组形心间的距离均为1.5a，2号、3号铆钉与铆钉组形心间的距离均为0.5a，因此1号铆钉和4号铆钉承担的水平向剪力大于2号铆钉和3号铆钉承担的水平向剪力。将水平向剪力与竖直向剪力合成为铆钉承担的总剪力后可知，Q<sub>1</sub>＝Q<sub>4</sub>＞Q<sub>3</sub>＝Q<sub>2</sub>。	
1. 圆轴直径为d，剪切弹性模量为G，在外力作用下发生扭转变形，现测得单位长度扭转角为θ，圆轴的最大切应力是{{c1::（）}}。[2013、2010年真题]	"<img height=""40"" id=""图片 1"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0553c062-f8f0-44a4-a637-abd435f316ca.png"" width=""65""/><br><img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a83c8fd8-caca-4369-885b-5c12ecfb47e7.png"" width=""78""/><br><img height=""20"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1b7b2fdf-6f9d-4af3-bc82-e4312fb186d2.png"" width=""57""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4d1118ca-b144-4b84-8540-24ef5caf1063.png"" width=""58""/>"	D	"由公式<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/393bc513-c5da-4c93-af43-41c84a5a1433.jpg"" width=""47""/>得，T=θGI<sub>p</sub>，则最大切应力<img height=""44"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0e1092ad-76c8-46ef-b99f-ba4c45c21576.jpg"" width=""138""/>。"	
2. 在一套传动系统中，有多根圆轴，假设所有圆轴传递的功率相同，但转速不同。各轴所承受的扭矩与其转速的关系是{{c1::（）}}。[2014年真题]	转速快的轴扭矩大<br>转速慢的轴扭矩大<br>各轴的扭矩相同<br>无法确定	B	根据公式T=9550P/n可知，在功率相同的情况下转速慢的轴扭矩大。式中，T为扭矩（N·m）；P为功率（kW）；n为转速（r/min）；9550为常系数。	
"3. 图5-3-1所示两根圆轴，横载面面积相同但分别为实心圆和空心圆。在相同的扭矩T作用下，两轴最大切应力的关系是{{c1::（）}}。[2013年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""123"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/a7035a3b-cdb2-4340-a73d-3a01e305c555.png"" width=""620""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-3-1</span>"	τ<sub>a</sub>＜τ<sub>b</sub><br>τ<sub>a</sub>=τ<sub>b</sub><br>τ<sub>a</sub>＞τ<sub>b</sub><br>不能确定	C	"设d为实心圆直径，α=d/D，D为空心圆截面外径。由最大切应力公式<img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/aff1c888-8f02-46ee-88cb-48410a2a2d85.png"" width=""73""/>由两轴截面面积相等得：<img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c2437b75-6cdb-42cb-bd3f-89f6eff25940.jpg"" width=""250""/>，实心圆截面的抗扭截面系数W<sub>Ta</sub>=πd<sup>3</sup>/16；空心圆截面的W<sub>Tb</sub>=πD<sup>3</sup><sup>（</sup>1-α<sup>4</sup>）/16，因此两轴的抗扭截面系数之比为：<img height=""50"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0cd4d3c0-471e-4280-a9cd-c5c6de3bd312.jpg"" width=""393""/>，故τa＞τb。"	
4. 图示受扭空心圆轴横截面上的切应力分布图中，正确的是{{c1::（）}}。[2014、2011年真题]	"<img height=""97"" id=""图片 1558"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d29835b8-d8ed-48ed-9c71-189aa664c8f8.jpg"" width=""97""/><br><img height=""96"" id=""图片 1559"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/471a7e00-f5b7-470a-bffa-ba0668b4675d.jpg"" width=""102""/><br><img height=""96"" id=""图片 1560"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/13648b1d-48ca-4115-8d98-53a59114bb7d.jpg"" width=""106""/><br><img height=""102"" id=""图片 1561"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/43bba19b-7fc9-4041-ae6d-88dc20d5436f.jpg"" width=""102""/>"	B	受扭空心圆轴横截面上的切应力分布与半径成正比，而且在空心圆内径中无应力，只有B图是正确的。	
"5. 图5-3-2（a）所示圆轴抗扭截面模量为W<sub>t</sub>，切变模量为Ｇ，扭转变形后，圆轴表面A点处截取的单元体互相垂直的相邻边线改变了γ角，如图所（b）示。圆轴承受的扭矩Ｔ为{{c1::（）}}。[2009年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""121"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/1b46246a-400b-4561-a1c7-683b8718364f.png"" width=""345""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-3-2</span>"	"<img height=""21"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b4fb4576-2281-4573-b24d-68905773d342.png"" width=""60""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/18366ec3-cfe2-4c58-bfb6-65e542888394.png"" width=""49""/><br><img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d9eb227d-57ee-4080-8b7b-81175d690462.png"" width=""56""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/66bae043-ba87-4889-9054-baee68f5fbcb.png"" width=""48""/>"	A	根据剪应力计算公式τ=Gγ=T/W<sub>t</sub>，得T=GγW<sub>t</sub>。	
6. 直径为d的实心圆轴受扭，若使扭转角减小一半，圆轴的直径需变为{{c1::（）}}。[2012年真题]	"<img height=""23"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/554a0cab-8d08-4fea-bd1c-09c31f7964ef.jpg"" width=""28""/><br><img height=""21"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/82df4bee-2230-41aa-ab7a-9554a15f7ad5.jpg"" width=""25""/><br>0.5d<br>2d"	A	"由<img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/fbb539fd-b6a9-4f83-8ec7-127697bee13c.jpg"" width=""153""/>得IP<sub>1</sub>=2I<sub>p</sub>，所以<img height=""41"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/365829b9-eee7-497b-97b5-31e8cc4b31fc.jpg"" width=""187""/>。"

"8. 如图5-3-3所示，左端固定的直杆受扭转力偶作用，在截面1—1和2—2处的扭矩为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""115"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0ae5db65-20bc-4ecb-93b6-1bb6f5d55e2b.jpg"" width=""383""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-3-3</span>"	12.5kN·m，-3kN·m<br>-2.5kN·m，-3kN·m<br>-2.5kN·m，3kN·m<br>2.5kN·m，-3kN·m	D	用右手螺旋法则，大拇指指向截面为负，背离截面为正。截面2—2扭矩T=2-5=-3kN·m；截面1—1扭矩T=1+4.5+2-5=2.5 kN·m。

"10. 如图5-3-5所示，圆截面受扭杆件的直径为d，在B截面与C截面处分别作用大小为3T与T的外力偶矩，若T与3T的方向相反，则杆内的最大剪应力为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""118"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/3664b83c-eb7d-4d8b-8d51-2e649b24ed5c.jpg"" width=""328""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-3-5</span>"	"<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/eeeaa91d-63dd-4cf5-971e-c4b227895ef4.png"" width=""45""/><br><img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c2ba4da9-2112-44fa-a4d0-7aa1004a697e.png"" width=""48""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4a467e99-32e3-4839-a804-401aa615fe41.png"" width=""48""/><br><img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/289b2d75-36ee-43a0-a0b9-ff30cbca8cfb.png"" width=""46""/>"	B	"由截面法可知，图5-3-5所示圆杆内的最大扭矩出现在AB段，则最大剪应力也应出现在AB段内，其大小为：<img height=""60"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4cc930a7-2ebc-4bdb-8a3b-9af6f933afa2.jpg"" width=""199""/>。"	
11. 将圆轴的直径减小到原来的3/4，在其他条件不变的情况下，圆轴的单位长度扭角与轴内最大剪应力分别改变为原来的{{c1::（）}}。	"<img height=""36"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/09aa44d7-3623-4257-a8e2-47dcc4cfd6f0.png"" width=""49""/><br><img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7648be70-e5d2-4c12-961e-ac4786a9b632.png"" width=""47""/><br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/9b9d9e69-4b10-407a-8fcc-4d1fb0eceaaa.png"" width=""55""/><br><img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/0ab80707-d9e5-4709-ba3d-95deb35f7113.png"" width=""56""/>"	C	"当圆轴直径减小到原来的3/4时，极惯性矩<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/93dec6e1-ec89-4f92-bbc4-cc0167c61024.jpg"" width=""75""/>减小为原来的<img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/ceaac0b3-ab56-4f99-992d-4bcd0e2a0efd.jpg"" width=""25""/>，抗扭截面系数<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c907c919-51b8-40e7-87a4-315d35fe019a.jpg"" width=""79""/>减小为原来的<img height=""33"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/3fe77955-5346-46f8-82b9-d3e633628eda.jpg"" width=""20""/>。由于单位长度扭转角与极惯性矩成反比，因此，单位扭转角改变为原来的<img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/45ea9423-8ec6-4f74-b64f-b2bad4edb082.jpg"" width=""23""/>；由于最大剪应力与抗扭截面系数成反比，因此最大剪应力改变为原来的<img height=""31"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/4c95edb0-757f-4d06-b96d-5a878c6c0630.jpg"" width=""19""/>。"	
"12. 如图5-3-6所示当外力偶矩m作用在图示等直圆轴自由端时，自由端截面上的C点转动至C<sub>1</sub>处，且CC<sub>1</sub>＝1.5mm，已知圆轴材料的剪切弹性模量G＝8×10<sup>4</sup>MPa，则轴内最大剪应力大小为{{c1::（）}}MPa。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""115"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/679ab3b5-d4b4-48bc-8a2d-8671ff4d1d13.jpg"" width=""244""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-3-6</span>"	40<br>80<br>120<br>160	C	"剪应变<img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/5d80b2d7-363e-4226-a1d3-cdfc6556d01e.png"" width=""123""/>故最大剪应力τ<sub>max</sub>＝Gγ＝120MPa。"	
13. 两根同种材料制成的等长实心圆轴，端截面处均受到同样大小的扭矩作用，若第一根轴的直径是第二根轴直径的一半，则第一根轴的扭转角是第二根轴扭转角的{{c1::（）}}倍。	2<br>4<br>8<br>16	D	圆轴的扭转角与横截面极惯性矩成反比，而横截面极惯性矩与直径的四次方成正比，故圆轴的扭转角与横截面直径的四次方成反比。	
"14. 力偶矩m1＝7N·m与m<sup>2</sup>＝5N·m分别作用在如图5-3-7所示圆轴的B、C截面处，已知l＝50cm，直径d＝10mm，材料的剪切弹性模量G＝82GPa，则A、C两截面的相对扭转角为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""123"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/28ac5605-200f-406e-bb16-a0871cb8e19c.jpg"" width=""254""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-3-7</span>"	φ<sub>CA</sub>＝－1.42°<br>φ<sub>CA</sub>＝－1.07°<br>φ<sub>CA</sub>＝0.19°<br>φ<sub>CA</sub>＝2.49°	B	"AB段轴的扭矩为m<sub>1</sub>－m<sub>2</sub>，BC段轴的扭矩为－m<sub>2</sub>，因此C、B截面的相对扭转角<img height=""50"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/c7a7292c-e072-4d02-ad18-a45d6097f060.jpg"" width=""102""/>，B、A截面的相对扭转角<img height=""49"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/9b66c2f7-a949-4ed9-b00d-293a338345e6.png"" width=""133""/>。从而得圆轴A、C截面的相对扭转角为：<img height=""49"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/05f6a1ab-4ee3-47dd-a15e-9a85a10bc9cc.jpg"" width=""360""/>。"	
"15. 如图5-3-8所示铸铁材料制成的圆轴，在轴端力偶矩作用下，其破坏形式应为{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""94"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6895f9cb-5e85-46d5-bdb5-a01828676028.jpg"" width=""300""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-3-8</span>"	沿横截面Ⅰ—Ⅰ剪断<br>沿横截面Ⅰ—Ⅰ拉断<br>沿螺旋面Ⅱ（与试件轴线夹角45°）拉断<br>沿螺旋面Ⅲ（与试件轴线夹角45°）拉断	C	铸铁抗拉强度比抗压强度低得多，所以排除AB两项；考虑扭矩方向知C项正确。	
"16. 如图5-3-9所示，等截面传动轴上安装有三个齿轮，作用在每个齿轮上的外力偶矩一定，若想通过齿轮位置的改变使得传动轴内扭矩最小，则齿轮a应安装在{{c1::（）}}。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""121"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/2253a260-6478-469c-aa18-3dc6135fe901.jpg"" width=""310""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-3-9</span>"	轴的最左端<br>轴的最右端<br>齿轮b与c之间<br>任意截面处	C	传动轴上齿轮位置设计时，应尽量使主动轮靠近传动轴中心，以减小传动轴的扭矩。	
"17. 如图5-3-10所示传动轴转速n＝300r/min，主动轮A的输入功率P<sub>A</sub>＝10kW，从动轮B、C、D的输出功率分别为P<sub>B</sub>＝4.5kW，P<sub>C</sub>＝3.5kW，P<sub>D</sub>＝2kW，若传动轴材料的剪切弹性模量G＝80GPa，[τ]＝40MPa，则传动轴的直径为{{c1::（）}}mm。<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""114"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7a61d177-a09b-491a-a85a-6945c679756d.jpg"" width=""602""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-3-10</span>"	18<br>20<br>25<br>30	D	"由传动轴力偶矩计算式<img height=""40"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/d8808cf4-b7bf-4b77-823c-3726b5017056.png"" width=""75""/>可得，三个从动轮上的力偶矩分别为：m<sub>B</sub>＝143.24N·m，m<sub>C</sub>＝111.40N·m，m<sub>D</sub>＝63.66N·m。<br/>由此可得轴内最大扭矩T<sub>max</sub>＝m<sub>C</sub>+m<sub>D</sub>=175.06N·m，由强度条件<img height=""53"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/aa043b84-ae9e-4bf4-afda-32020456160c.jpg"" width=""210""/>，得：<img height=""50"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/8f7451d8-fc7c-4205-9add-ae218c884132.png"" width=""152""/>因此传动轴的直径应为30mm。"

"2. 图5-4-2所示矩形截面对z<sub>1</sub>轴的惯性矩I<sub>z1</sub>为{{c1::（）}}。[2010年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""269"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f64346ef-24bd-455a-a26c-0e5a55360d22.jpg"" width=""224""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-4-2</span>"	"<img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/e75de3b0-cfda-461e-9626-3743a25a36ef.png"" width=""61""/><br><img height=""39"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/dc733189-60be-4558-8684-30a5cda00d0f.png"" width=""59""/><br><img height=""37"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/dde0bfbe-9c3a-4789-826c-b8e34c1c8d97.png"" width=""68""/><br><img height=""38"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/f4764261-a98e-47aa-95cf-1f564e337adb.png"" width=""71""/>"	D	"首先求出该矩形截面对z轴的截面惯性矩<img height=""35"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/7f897802-0e0a-4358-aba9-a64317ebcb1f.jpg"" width=""51""/>，再利用平行移轴定理得：<img height=""47"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/b6c9a45f-23c7-4d05-b07d-faadb76767df.jpg"" width=""246""/>。"	
"3. 梁的横截面可选用图5-4-3所示空心矩形、矩形、正方形和圆形四种之一，假设四种截面的面积均相等，载荷作用方向铅垂向下，承载能力最大的截面是{{c1::（）}}。[2014年真题]<br/><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;""><img height=""169"" src=""http://admintk.100xuexi.com/UpLoadImage/2013-05-07/6441eae2-3642-48e9-a0f2-bf6d523b748d.png"" width=""486""/></span><span style=""display:block;text-align:center;"">图5-4-3</span>"	空心矩形<br>实心矩形<br>正方形<br>圆形	A	由梁的正应力强度条件可知，梁的承载能力与梁横截面惯性矩I（或W）的大小成正比，在外荷载产生的弯矩不变的情况下，截面惯性矩（或W）越大，其承载能力也越大，显然相同面积制成的梁，矩形比圆形好，空心矩形的惯性矩（或W）最大，其承载能力最大。
